incomes_NNS will_MD be_VB crucial_JJ as_IN the_DT population_NN ages_NNS because_IN a_DT relatively_RB
smaller_JJR workforce_NN will_MD bear_VB the_DT burden_NN of_IN financing_NN Social_NNP Security_NNP

services_NNS in_IN the_DT United_NNP States_NNPS (_( GDP_NNP )_) ._.
The_DT model_NN incorporates_VBZ a_DT simple_JJ representation_NN of_IN net_JJ financial_JJ
flows_NNS between_IN the_DT U_NNP ._. S_NNP ._. economy_NN and_CC the_DT rest_NN of_IN the_DT world_NN ._.
Essentially_RB the_DT rest_NN of_IN the_DT world_NN is_VBZ treated_VBN as_IN analogous_JJ to_TO a_DT bank_NN
where_WRB the_DT United_NNP States_NNPS can_MD make_VB deposits_NNS or_CC withdrawals_NNS or_CC draw_VB on_IN
a_DT credit_NN line_NN ._. Every_DT year_NN there_EX are_VBP income_NN flows_NNS to_TO or_CC from_IN this_DT

(_( NIIP_NNP )_) of_IN the_DT United_NNP States_NNPS ,_, which_WDT generates_VBZ a_DT net_JJ flow_NN of_IN income_NN

A_DT key_NN model_NN assumption_NN affecting_VBG international_JJ flows_NNS is_VBZ the_DT

around_IN its_PRP$ longterm_JJ trend_NN ._. We_PRP assume_VBP that_IN net_JJ foreign_JJ investment_NN

33_CD ._. 3_LS cents_NNS in_IN foreign_JJ investment_NN in_IN the_DT United_NNP States_NNPS ._. Our_PRP$
Budget_NNP and_CC Other_NNP Assumptions_NNP
assumption_NN is_VBZ consistent_JJ with_IN the_DT strong_JJ correlation_NN between_IN
